| `vacuum_max_eager_freeze_failure_rate`  | [18](../param-autovacuum.md?pivots=postgresql-18#vacuum_max_eager_freeze_failure_rate)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 | Fraction of pages in a relation vacuum can scan and fail to freeze before disabling eager scanning. A value of 0.0 disables eager scanning and a value of 1.0 will eagerly scan up to 100 percent of the all-visible pages in the relation. If vacuum successfully freezes these pages, the cap is lower than 100 percent, because the goal is to amortize page freezing across multiple vacuums.|

| `unix_socket_directories`        | [11](../param-connections-authentication-connection-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-11#unix_socket_directories), [12](../param-connections-authentication-connection-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-12#unix_socket_directories), [13](../param-connections-authentication-connection-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-13#unix_socket_directories), [14](../param-connections-authentication-connection-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-14#unix_socket_directories), [15](../param-connections-authentication-connection-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-15#unix_socket_directories), [16](../param-connections-authentication-connection-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-16#unix_socket_directories), [17](../param-connections-authentication-connection-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-17#unix_socket_directories), [18](../param-connections-authentication-connection-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-18#unix_socket_directories)                                                         | Sets the directories where Unix-domain sockets will be created.|
| `unix_socket_group`              | [11](../param-connections-authentication-connection-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-11#unix_socket_group), [12](../param-connections-authentication-connection-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-12#unix_socket_group), [13](../param-connections-authentication-connection-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-13#unix_socket_group), [14](../param-connections-authentication-connection-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-14#unix_socket_group), [15](../param-connections-authentication-connection-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-15#unix_socket_group), [16](../param-connections-authentication-connection-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-16#unix_socket_group), [17](../param-connections-authentication-connection-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-17#unix_socket_group), [18](../param-connections-authentication-connection-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-18#unix_socket_group)                                                                                                         | Sets the owning group of the Unix-domain socket. The owning user of the socket is always the user that starts the server.|
| `unix_socket_permissions`        | [11](../param-connections-authentication-connection-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-11#unix_socket_permissions), [12](../param-connections-authentication-connection-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-12#unix_socket_permissions), [13](../param-connections-authentication-connection-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-13#unix_socket_permissions), [14](../param-connections-authentication-connection-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-14#unix_socket_permissions), [15](../param-connections-authentication-connection-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-15#unix_socket_permissions), [16](../param-connections-authentication-connection-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-16#unix_socket_permissions), [17](../param-connections-authentication-connection-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-17#unix_socket_permissions), [18](../param-connections-authentication-connection-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-18#unix_socket_permissions)                                                         | Sets the access permissions of the Unix-domain socket. Unix-domain sockets use the usual Unix file system permission set. The parameter value is expected to be a numeric mode specification in the form accepted by the chmod and umask system calls. (To use the customary octal format the number must start with a 0 (zero).).|

This setting should generally be left disabled but may be useful for debugging or other purposes.|
| `pgaudit.log_level`                             | [11](../param-customized-options.md?pivots=postgresql-11#pgauditlog_level), [12](../param-customized-options.md?pivots=postgresql-12#pgauditlog_level), [13](../param-customized-options.md?pivots=postgresql-13#pgauditlog_level), [14](../param-customized-options.md?pivots=postgresql-14#pgauditlog_level), [15](../param-customized-options.md?pivots=postgresql-15#pgauditlog_level), [16](../param-customized-options.md?pivots=postgresql-16#pgauditlog_level), [17](../param-customized-options.md?pivots=postgresql-17#pgauditlog_level), [18](../param-customized-options.md?pivots=postgresql-18#pgauditlog_level)                                                                                                                                                                                                         | Specifies the log level that will be used for log entries. This setting is used for regression testing and may also be useful to end users for testing or other purposes. It is not intended to be used in a production environment as it may leak which statements are being logged to the user.|
| `pgaudit.log_parameter`                         | [11](../param-customized-options.md?pivots=postgresql-11#pgauditlog_parameter), [12](../param-customized-options.md?pivots=postgresql-12#pgauditlog_parameter), [13](../param-customized-options.md?pivots=postgresql-13#pgauditlog_parameter), [14](../param-customized-options.md?pivots=postgresql-14#pgauditlog_parameter), [15](../param-customized-options.md?pivots=postgresql-15#pgauditlog_parameter), [16](../param-customized-options.md?pivots=postgresql-16#pgauditlog_parameter), [17](../param-customized-options.md?pivots=postgresql-17#pgauditlog_parameter), [18](../param-customized-options.md?pivots=postgresql-18#pgauditlog_parameter)                                                                                                                                                                         | Specifies that audit logging should include the parameters that were passed with the statement. If 0 (the default), parameters are not checked for size. If set, when the size of the parameter is longer than the setting, the value in the audit log is replaced with a placeholder. Note that for character types, the length is in bytes for the parameter's encoding, not characters.|
| `pgaudit.log_relation`                          | [11](../param-customized-options.md?pivots=postgresql-11#pgauditlog_relation), [12](../param-customized-options.md?pivots=postgresql-12#pgauditlog_relation), [13](../param-customized-options.md?pivots=postgresql-13#pgauditlog_relation), [14](../param-customized-options.md?pivots=postgresql-14#pgauditlog_relation), [15](../param-customized-options.md?pivots=postgresql-15#pgauditlog_relation), [16](../param-customized-options.md?pivots=postgresql-16#pgauditlog_relation), [17](../param-customized-options.md?pivots=postgresql-17#pgauditlog_relation), [18](../param-customized-options.md?pivots=postgresql-18#pgauditlog_relation)                                                                                                                                                                                 | Specifies whether session audit logging should create a separate log entry for each relation referenced in a SELECT or DML statement. Modifies behaviour of pg_failover_slots.standby_slot_names so to allow logical replication of a transaction after at least pg_failover_slots.standby_slots_min_confirmed physical peers have confirmed the transaction as durably flushed. The value -1 (default) means all entries in pg_failover_slots.standby_slot_namesmust confirm the write. The value 0 causes pg_failover_slots.standby_slots_min_confirmedto be effectively ignored.|

| `timescaledb.disable_load`                      | [12](../param-customized-options.md?pivots=postgresql-12#timescaledbdisable_load), [13](../param-customized-options.md?pivots=postgresql-13#timescaledbdisable_load), [14](../param-customized-options.md?pivots=postgresql-14#timescaledbdisable_load), [15](../param-customized-options.md?pivots=postgresql-15#timescaledbdisable_load), [16](../param-customized-options.md?pivots=postgresql-16#timescaledbdisable_load), [17](../param-customized-options.md?pivots=postgresql-17#timescaledbdisable_load)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       | Disable the loading of the actual extension.|

On the publisher, it allows streaming or serializing each change in logical decoding. On the subscriber, it allows serialization of all changes to files and notifies the parallel apply workers to read and apply them at the end of the transaction.|
| `debug_parallel_query`                | [16](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-16#debug_parallel_query), [17](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-17#debug_parallel_query), [18](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-18#debug_parallel_query)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            | Forces the planner's use parallel query nodes. This can be useful for testing the parallel query infrastructure by forcing the planner to generate plans that contain nodes that perform tuple communication between workers and the main process.|

| `ignore_checksum_failure`             | [11](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-11#ignore_checksum_failure), [12](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-12#ignore_checksum_failure), [13](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-13#ignore_checksum_failure), [14](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-14#ignore_checksum_failure), [15](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-15#ignore_checksum_failure), [16](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-16#ignore_checksum_failure), [17](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-17#ignore_checksum_failure), [18](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-18#ignore_checksum_failure)                         | Continues processing after a checksum failure. Detection of a checksum failure normally causes PostgreSQL to report an error, aborting the current transaction. Setting ignore_checksum_failure to true causes the system to ignore the failure (but still report a warning), and continue processing. This behavior could cause crashes or other serious problems. Only has an effect if checksums are enabled.|
| `ignore_invalid_pages`                | [13](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-13#ignore_invalid_pages), [14](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-14#ignore_invalid_pages), [15](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-15#ignore_invalid_pages), [16](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-16#ignore_invalid_pages), [17](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-17#ignore_invalid_pages), [18](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-18#ignore_invalid_pages)                                                                                                                                                                                                               | Continues recovery after an invalid pages failure. Detection of WAL records having references to invalid pages during recovery causes PostgreSQL to raise a PANIC-level error, aborting the recovery. Setting \"ignore_invalid_pages\" to true causes the system to ignore invalid page references in WAL records (but still report a warning), and continue recovery. This behavior may cause crashes, data loss, propagate or hide corruption, or other serious problems. Only has an effect during recovery or in standby mode.|
| `ignore_system_indexes`               | [11](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-11#ignore_system_indexes), [12](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-12#ignore_system_indexes), [13](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-13#ignore_system_indexes), [14](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-14#ignore_system_indexes), [15](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-15#ignore_system_indexes), [16](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-16#ignore_system_indexes), [17](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-17#ignore_system_indexes), [18](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-18#ignore_system_indexes)                                         | Disables reading from system indexes. It does not prevent updating the indexes, so it is safe to use. The worst consequence is slowness.|
| `jit_debugging_support`               | [11](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-11#jit_debugging_support), [12](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-12#jit_debugging_support), [13](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-13#jit_debugging_support), [14](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-14#jit_debugging_support), [15](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-15#jit_debugging_support), [16](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-16#jit_debugging_support), [17](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-17#jit_debugging_support), [18](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-18#jit_debugging_support)                                         | Register JIT-compiled functions with debugger.|
| `jit_dump_bitcode`                    | [11](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-11#jit_dump_bitcode), [12](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-12#jit_dump_bitcode), [13](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-13#jit_dump_bitcode), [14](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-14#jit_dump_bitcode), [15](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-15#jit_dump_bitcode), [16](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-16#jit_dump_bitcode), [17](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-17#jit_dump_bitcode), [18](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-18#jit_dump_bitcode)                                                                                 | Write out LLVM bitcode to facilitate JIT debugging.|

| `send_abort_for_crash`                | [16](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-16#send_abort_for_crash), [17](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-17#send_abort_for_crash), [18](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-18#send_abort_for_crash)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            | Send SIGABRT not SIGQUIT to child processes after backend crash.|
| `send_abort_for_kill`                 | [16](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-16#send_abort_for_kill), [17](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-17#send_abort_for_kill), [18](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-18#send_abort_for_kill)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               | Send SIGABRT not SIGKILL to stuck child processes.|
| `trace_connection_negotiation`        | [17](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-17#trace_connection_negotiation), [18](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-18#trace_connection_negotiation)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           | Logs details of pre-authentication connection handshake.|
| `trace_notify`                        | [11](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-11#trace_notify), [12](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-12#trace_notify), [13](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-13#trace_notify), [14](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-14#trace_notify), [15](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-15#trace_notify), [16](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-16#trace_notify), [17](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-17#trace_notify), [18](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-18#trace_notify)                                                                                                                 | Generates debugging output for LISTEN and NOTIFY.|
| `trace_recovery_messages`             | [11](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-11#trace_recovery_messages), [12](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-12#trace_recovery_messages), [13](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-13#trace_recovery_messages), [14](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-14#trace_recovery_messages), [15](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-15#trace_recovery_messages), [16](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-16#trace_recovery_messages)                                                                                                                                                                                             | Enables logging of recovery-related debugging information.|
| `trace_sort`                          | [11](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-11#trace_sort), [12](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-12#trace_sort), [13](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-13#trace_sort), [14](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-14#trace_sort), [15](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-15#trace_sort), [16](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-16#trace_sort), [17](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-17#trace_sort), [18](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-18#trace_sort)                                                                                                                                 | Emit information about resource usage in sorting.|
| `wal_consistency_checking`            | [11](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-11#wal_consistency_checking), [12](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-12#wal_consistency_checking), [13](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-13#wal_consistency_checking), [14](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-14#wal_consistency_checking), [15](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-15#wal_consistency_checking), [16](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-16#wal_consistency_checking), [17](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-17#wal_consistency_checking), [18](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-18#wal_consistency_checking)                 | Sets the WAL resource managers for which WAL consistency checks are done. Full-page images will be logged for all data blocks and cross-checked against the results of WAL replay.|
| `zero_damaged_pages`                  | [11](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-11#zero_damaged_pages), [12](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-12#zero_damaged_pages), [13](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-13#zero_damaged_pages), [14](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-14#zero_damaged_pages), [15](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-15#zero_damaged_pages), [16](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-16#zero_damaged_pages), [17](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-17#zero_damaged_pages), [18](../param-developer-options.md?pivots=postgresql-18#zero_damaged_pages)                                                                 | Continues processing past damaged page headers. Detection of a damaged page header normally causes PostgreSQL to report an error, aborting the current transaction. Setting \"zero_damaged_pages\" to true causes the system to instead report a warning, zero out the damaged page, and continue processing. This behavior will destroy data, namely all the rows on the damaged page.|

### Lock Management



|               Name               |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        Versions                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |                                                                                                                            Description                                                                                                                            |
|----------------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `deadlock_timeout`               | [11](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-11#deadlock_timeout), [12](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-12#deadlock_timeout), [13](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-13#deadlock_timeout), [14](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-14#deadlock_timeout), [15](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-15#deadlock_timeout), [16](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-16#deadlock_timeout), [17](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-17#deadlock_timeout), [18](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-18#deadlock_timeout)                                                                                                                 | Sets the time to wait on a lock before checking for deadlock.|
| `max_locks_per_transaction`      | [11](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-11#max_locks_per_transaction), [12](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-12#max_locks_per_transaction), [13](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-13#max_locks_per_transaction), [14](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-14#max_locks_per_transaction), [15](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-15#max_locks_per_transaction), [16](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-16#max_locks_per_transaction), [17](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-17#max_locks_per_transaction), [18](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-18#max_locks_per_transaction)                                         | Sets the maximum number of locks per transaction. The shared lock table is sized on the assumption that at most \"max_locks_per_transaction\" objects per server process or prepared transaction will need to be locked at any one time.|
| `max_pred_locks_per_page`        | [11](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-11#max_pred_locks_per_page), [12](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-12#max_pred_locks_per_page), [13](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-13#max_pred_locks_per_page), [14](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-14#max_pred_locks_per_page), [15](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-15#max_pred_locks_per_page), [16](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-16#max_pred_locks_per_page), [17](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-17#max_pred_locks_per_page), [18](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-18#max_pred_locks_per_page)                                                         | Sets the maximum number of predicate-locked tuples per page. If more than this number of tuples on the same page are locked by a connection, those locks are replaced by a page-level lock.|
| `max_pred_locks_per_relation`    | [11](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-11#max_pred_locks_per_relation), [12](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-12#max_pred_locks_per_relation), [13](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-13#max_pred_locks_per_relation), [14](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-14#max_pred_locks_per_relation), [15](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-15#max_pred_locks_per_relation), [16](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-16#max_pred_locks_per_relation), [17](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-17#max_pred_locks_per_relation), [18](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-18#max_pred_locks_per_relation)                         | Sets the maximum number of predicate-locked pages and tuples per relation. If more than this total of pages and tuples in the same relation are locked by a connection, those locks are replaced by a relation-level lock.|
| `max_pred_locks_per_transaction` | [11](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-11#max_pred_locks_per_transaction), [12](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-12#max_pred_locks_per_transaction), [13](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-13#max_pred_locks_per_transaction), [14](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-14#max_pred_locks_per_transaction), [15](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-15#max_pred_locks_per_transaction), [16](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-16#max_pred_locks_per_transaction), [17](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-17#max_pred_locks_per_transaction), [18](../param-lock-management.md?pivots=postgresql-18#max_pred_locks_per_transaction) | Sets the maximum number of predicate locks per transaction. The shared predicate lock table is sized on the assumption that at most \"max_pred_locks_per_transaction\" objects per server process or prepared transaction will need to be locked at any one time.|

| `pgbouncer.server_idle_timeout`       | [11](../param-pgbouncer.md?pivots=postgresql-11#pgbouncerserver_idle_timeout), [12](../param-pgbouncer.md?pivots=postgresql-12#pgbouncerserver_idle_timeout), [13](../param-pgbouncer.md?pivots=postgresql-13#pgbouncerserver_idle_timeout), [14](../param-pgbouncer.md?pivots=postgresql-14#pgbouncerserver_idle_timeout), [15](../param-pgbouncer.md?pivots=postgresql-15#pgbouncerserver_idle_timeout), [16](../param-pgbouncer.md?pivots=postgresql-16#pgbouncerserver_idle_timeout), [17](../param-pgbouncer.md?pivots=postgresql-17#pgbouncerserver_idle_timeout), [18](../param-pgbouncer.md?pivots=postgresql-18#pgbouncerserver_idle_timeout)                                                 | If a server connection has been idle more than this many seconds it will be dropped. If 0 then timeout is disabled.|
| `pgbouncer.stats_users`               | [11](../param-pgbouncer.md?pivots=postgresql-11#pgbouncerstats_users), [12](../param-pgbouncer.md?pivots=postgresql-12#pgbouncerstats_users), [13](../param-pgbouncer.md?pivots=postgresql-13#pgbouncerstats_users), [14](../param-pgbouncer.md?pivots=postgresql-14#pgbouncerstats_users), [15](../param-pgbouncer.md?pivots=postgresql-15#pgbouncerstats_users), [16](../param-pgbouncer.md?pivots=postgresql-16#pgbouncerstats_users), [17](../param-pgbouncer.md?pivots=postgresql-17#pgbouncerstats_users), [18](../param-pgbouncer.md?pivots=postgresql-18#pgbouncerstats_users)                                                                                                                 | Comma-separated list of database users that are allowed to connect and run read-only queries on the pgBouncer console.|

| `geqo_seed`           | [11](../param-query-tuning-genetic-query-optimizer.md?pivots=postgresql-11#geqo_seed), [12](../param-query-tuning-genetic-query-optimizer.md?pivots=postgresql-12#geqo_seed), [13](../param-query-tuning-genetic-query-optimizer.md?pivots=postgresql-13#geqo_seed), [14](../param-query-tuning-genetic-query-optimizer.md?pivots=postgresql-14#geqo_seed), [15](../param-query-tuning-genetic-query-optimizer.md?pivots=postgresql-15#geqo_seed), [16](../param-query-tuning-genetic-query-optimizer.md?pivots=postgresql-16#geqo_seed), [17](../param-query-tuning-genetic-query-optimizer.md?pivots=postgresql-17#geqo_seed), [18](../param-query-tuning-genetic-query-optimizer.md?pivots=postgresql-18#geqo_seed)                                                                                 | GEQO: seed for random path selection.|
| `geqo_selection_bias` | [11](../param-query-tuning-genetic-query-optimizer.md?pivots=postgresql-11#geqo_selection_bias), [12](../param-query-tuning-genetic-query-optimizer.md?pivots=postgresql-12#geqo_selection_bias), [13](../param-query-tuning-genetic-query-optimizer.md?pivots=postgresql-13#geqo_selection_bias), [14](../param-query-tuning-genetic-query-optimizer.md?pivots=postgresql-14#geqo_selection_bias), [15](../param-query-tuning-genetic-query-optimizer.md?pivots=postgresql-15#geqo_selection_bias), [16](../param-query-tuning-genetic-query-optimizer.md?pivots=postgresql-16#geqo_selection_bias), [17](../param-query-tuning-genetic-query-optimizer.md?pivots=postgresql-17#geqo_selection_bias), [18](../param-query-tuning-genetic-query-optimizer.md?pivots=postgresql-18#geqo_selection_bias) | GEQO: selective pressure within the population.|
| `geqo_threshold`      | [11](../param-query-tuning-genetic-query-optimizer.md?pivots=postgresql-11#geqo_threshold), [12](../param-query-tuning-genetic-query-optimizer.md?pivots=postgresql-12#geqo_threshold), [13](../param-query-tuning-genetic-query-optimizer.md?pivots=postgresql-13#geqo_threshold), [14](../param-query-tuning-genetic-query-optimizer.md?pivots=postgresql-14#geqo_threshold), [15](../param-query-tuning-genetic-query-optimizer.md?pivots=postgresql-15#geqo_threshold), [16](../param-query-tuning-genetic-query-optimizer.md?pivots=postgresql-16#geqo_threshold), [17](../param-query-tuning-genetic-query-optimizer.md?pivots=postgresql-17#geqo_threshold), [18](../param-query-tuning-genetic-query-optimizer.md?pivots=postgresql-18#geqo_threshold)                                         | Sets the threshold of FROM items beyond which GEQO is used.|

|             Name             |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        Versions                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |                                                                                                         Description                                                                                                          |
|------------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `constraint_exclusion`       | [11](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-11#constraint_exclusion), [12](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-12#constraint_exclusion), [13](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-13#constraint_exclusion), [14](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-14#constraint_exclusion), [15](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-15#constraint_exclusion), [16](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-16#constraint_exclusion), [17](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-17#constraint_exclusion), [18](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-18#constraint_exclusion)                                         | Enables the planner to use constraints to optimize queries. Table scans will be skipped if their constraints guarantee that no rows match the query.|
| `cursor_tuple_fraction`      | [11](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-11#cursor_tuple_fraction), [12](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-12#cursor_tuple_fraction), [13](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-13#cursor_tuple_fraction), [14](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-14#cursor_tuple_fraction), [15](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-15#cursor_tuple_fraction), [16](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-16#cursor_tuple_fraction), [17](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-17#cursor_tuple_fraction), [18](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-18#cursor_tuple_fraction)                                 | Sets the planner's estimate of the fraction of a cursor's rows that will be retrieved.|
| `default_statistics_target`  | [11](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-11#default_statistics_target), [12](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-12#default_statistics_target), [13](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-13#default_statistics_target), [14](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-14#default_statistics_target), [15](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-15#default_statistics_target), [16](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-16#default_statistics_target), [17](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-17#default_statistics_target), [18](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-18#default_statistics_target) | Sets the default statistics target. This applies to table columns that have not had a column-specific target set via ALTER TABLE SET STATISTICS.|
| `from_collapse_limit`        | [11](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-11#from_collapse_limit), [12](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-12#from_collapse_limit), [13](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-13#from_collapse_limit), [14](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-14#from_collapse_limit), [15](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-15#from_collapse_limit), [16](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-16#from_collapse_limit), [17](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-17#from_collapse_limit), [18](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-18#from_collapse_limit)                                                 | Sets the FROM-list size beyond which subqueries are not collapsed. The planner will merge subqueries into upper queries if the resulting FROM list would have no more than this many items.|
| `jit`                        | [11](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-11#jit), [12](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-12#jit), [13](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-13#jit), [14](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-14#jit), [15](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-15#jit), [16](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-16#jit), [17](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-17#jit), [18](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-18#jit)                                                                                                                                                                                 | Allow JIT compilation.|
| `join_collapse_limit`        | [11](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-11#join_collapse_limit), [12](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-12#join_collapse_limit), [13](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-13#join_collapse_limit), [14](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-14#join_collapse_limit), [15](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-15#join_collapse_limit), [16](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-16#join_collapse_limit), [17](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-17#join_collapse_limit), [18](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-18#join_collapse_limit)                                                 | Sets the FROM-list size beyond which JOIN constructs are not flattened. The planner will flatten explicit JOIN constructs into lists of FROM items whenever a list of no more than this many items would result.|
| `plan_cache_mode`            | [12](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-12#plan_cache_mode), [13](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-13#plan_cache_mode), [14](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-14#plan_cache_mode), [15](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-15#plan_cache_mode), [16](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-16#plan_cache_mode), [17](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-17#plan_cache_mode), [18](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-18#plan_cache_mode)                                                                                                                                                                      | Controls the planner's selection of custom or generic plan. Prepared statements can have custom and generic plans, and the planner will attempt to choose which is better. This can be set to override the default behavior.|
| `recursive_worktable_factor` | [15](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-15#recursive_worktable_factor), [16](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-16#recursive_worktable_factor), [17](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-17#recursive_worktable_factor), [18](../param-query-tuning-planner-options.md?pivots=postgresql-18#recursive_worktable_factor)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         | Sets the planner's estimate of the average size of a recursive query's working table.|

| `jit_inline_above_cost`        | [11](../param-query-tuning-planner-cost-constants.md?pivots=postgresql-11#jit_inline_above_cost), [12](../param-query-tuning-planner-cost-constants.md?pivots=postgresql-12#jit_inline_above_cost), [13](../param-query-tuning-planner-cost-constants.md?pivots=postgresql-13#jit_inline_above_cost), [14](../param-query-tuning-planner-cost-constants.md?pivots=postgresql-14#jit_inline_above_cost), [15](../param-query-tuning-planner-cost-constants.md?pivots=postgresql-15#jit_inline_above_cost), [16](../param-query-tuning-planner-cost-constants.md?pivots=postgresql-16#jit_inline_above_cost), [17](../param-query-tuning-planner-cost-constants.md?pivots=postgresql-17#jit_inline_above_cost), [18](../param-query-tuning-planner-cost-constants.md?pivots=postgresql-18#jit_inline_above_cost)                                                         | Perform JIT inlining if query is more expensive. -1 disables inlining.|

| `min_parallel_index_scan_size` | [11](../param-query-tuning-planner-cost-constants.md?pivots=postgresql-11#min_parallel_index_scan_size), [12](../param-query-tuning-planner-cost-constants.md?pivots=postgresql-12#min_parallel_index_scan_size), [13](../param-query-tuning-planner-cost-constants.md?pivots=postgresql-13#min_parallel_index_scan_size), [14](../param-query-tuning-planner-cost-constants.md?pivots=postgresql-14#min_parallel_index_scan_size), [15](../param-query-tuning-planner-cost-constants.md?pivots=postgresql-15#min_parallel_index_scan_size), [16](../param-query-tuning-planner-cost-constants.md?pivots=postgresql-16#min_parallel_index_scan_size), [17](../param-query-tuning-planner-cost-constants.md?pivots=postgresql-17#min_parallel_index_scan_size), [18](../param-query-tuning-planner-cost-constants.md?pivots=postgresql-18#min_parallel_index_scan_size) | Sets the minimum amount of index data for a parallel scan. | `parallel_tuple_cost`          | [11](../param-query-tuning-planner-cost-constants.md?pivots=postgresql-11#parallel_tuple_cost), [12](../param-query-tuning-planner-cost-constants.md?pivots=postgresql-12#parallel_tuple_cost), [13](../param-query-tuning-planner-cost-constants.md?pivots=postgresql-13#parallel_tuple_cost), [14](../param-query-tuning-planner-cost-constants.md?pivots=postgresql-14#parallel_tuple_cost), [15](../param-query-tuning-planner-cost-constants.md?pivots=postgresql-15#parallel_tuple_cost), [16](../param-query-tuning-planner-cost-constants.md?pivots=postgresql-16#parallel_tuple_cost), [17](../param-query-tuning-planner-cost-constants.md?pivots=postgresql-17#parallel_tuple_cost), [18](../param-query-tuning-planner-cost-constants.md?pivots=postgresql-18#parallel_tuple_cost)                                                                         | Sets the planner's estimate of the cost of passing each tuple (row) from worker to leader backend.|

### Query Tuning / Planner Method Configuration

| `max_slot_wal_keep_size` | [13](../param-replication-sending-servers.md?pivots=postgresql-13#max_slot_wal_keep_size), [14](../param-replication-sending-servers.md?pivots=postgresql-14#max_slot_wal_keep_size), [15](../param-replication-sending-servers.md?pivots=postgresql-15#max_slot_wal_keep_size), [16](../param-replication-sending-servers.md?pivots=postgresql-16#max_slot_wal_keep_size), [17](../param-replication-sending-servers.md?pivots=postgresql-17#max_slot_wal_keep_size), [18](../param-replication-sending-servers.md?pivots=postgresql-18#max_slot_wal_keep_size)                                                                                                                                                                                       | Sets the maximum WAL size that can be reserved by replication slots. | `max_wal_senders`        | [11](../param-replication-sending-servers.md?pivots=postgresql-11#max_wal_senders), [12](../param-replication-sending-servers.md?pivots=postgresql-12#max_wal_senders), [13](../param-replication-sending-servers.md?pivots=postgresql-13#max_wal_senders), [14](../param-replication-sending-servers.md?pivots=postgresql-14#max_wal_senders), [15](../param-replication-sending-servers.md?pivots=postgresql-15#max_wal_senders), [16](../param-replication-sending-servers.md?pivots=postgresql-16#max_wal_senders), [17](../param-replication-sending-servers.md?pivots=postgresql-17#max_wal_senders), [18](../param-replication-sending-servers.md?pivots=postgresql-18#max_wal_senders)                                                         | Sets the maximum number of simultaneously running WAL sender processes.|

### Reporting and Logging / When to Log



|              Name               |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    Versions                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |                                                                                              Description                                                                                              |
|---------------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `log_min_duration_sample`       | [13](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-13#log_min_duration_sample), [14](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-14#log_min_duration_sample), [15](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-15#log_min_duration_sample), [16](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-16#log_min_duration_sample), [17](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-17#log_min_duration_sample), [18](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-18#log_min_duration_sample)                                                                                                                                                                                                               | Sets the minimum execution time above which a sample of statements will be logged. Sampling is determined by log_statement_sample_rate. Zero logs a sample of all queries. -1 turns this feature off.|
| `log_min_duration_statement`    | [11](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-11#log_min_duration_statement), [12](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-12#log_min_duration_statement), [13](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-13#log_min_duration_statement), [14](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-14#log_min_duration_statement), [15](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-15#log_min_duration_statement), [16](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-16#log_min_duration_statement), [17](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-17#log_min_duration_statement), [18](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-18#log_min_duration_statement) | Sets the minimum execution time above which all statements will be logged. Zero prints all queries. -1 turns this feature off.|
| `log_min_error_statement`       | [11](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-11#log_min_error_statement), [12](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-12#log_min_error_statement), [13](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-13#log_min_error_statement), [14](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-14#log_min_error_statement), [15](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-15#log_min_error_statement), [16](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-16#log_min_error_statement), [17](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-17#log_min_error_statement), [18](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-18#log_min_error_statement)                         | Causes all statements generating error at or above this level to be logged. Each level includes all the levels that follow it. The later the level, the fewer messages are sent.|
| `log_min_messages`              | [11](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-11#log_min_messages), [12](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-12#log_min_messages), [13](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-13#log_min_messages), [14](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-14#log_min_messages), [15](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-15#log_min_messages), [16](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-16#log_min_messages), [17](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-17#log_min_messages), [18](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-18#log_min_messages)                                                                                 | Sets the message levels that are logged. Each level includes all the levels that follow it. The later the level, the fewer messages are sent.|
| `log_startup_progress_interval` | [15](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-15#log_startup_progress_interval), [16](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-16#log_startup_progress_interval), [17](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-17#log_startup_progress_interval), [18](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-18#log_startup_progress_interval)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             | Time between progress updates for long-running startup operations. 0 turns this feature off.|
| `log_statement_sample_rate`     | [13](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-13#log_statement_sample_rate), [14](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-14#log_statement_sample_rate), [15](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-15#log_statement_sample_rate), [16](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-16#log_statement_sample_rate), [17](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-17#log_statement_sample_rate), [18](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-18#log_statement_sample_rate)                                                                                                                                                                                                   | Fraction of statements exceeding \"log_min_duration_sample\" to be logged. Use a value between 0.0 (never log) and 1.0 (always log).|
| `log_transaction_sample_rate`   | [12](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-12#log_transaction_sample_rate), [13](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-13#log_transaction_sample_rate), [14](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-14#log_transaction_sample_rate), [15](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-15#log_transaction_sample_rate), [16](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-16#log_transaction_sample_rate), [17](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-17#log_transaction_sample_rate), [18](../param-reporting-logging-when-log.md?pivots=postgresql-18#log_transaction_sample_rate)                                                                                        | Sets the fraction of transactions from which to log all statements. Use a value between 0.0 (never log) and 1.0 (log all statements for all transactions).|



### Reporting and Logging / Where to Log



|            Name            |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                Versions                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |                                                                                                                    Description                                                                                                                    |
|----------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `event_source`             | [11](../param-reporting-logging-where-log.md?pivots=postgresql-11#event_source), [12](../param-reporting-logging-where-log.md?pivots=postgresql-12#event_source), [13](../param-reporting-logging-where-log.md?pivots=postgresql-13#event_source), [14](../param-reporting-logging-where-log.md?pivots=postgresql-14#event_source), [15](../param-reporting-logging-where-log.md?pivots=postgresql-15#event_source), [16](../param-reporting-logging-where-log.md?pivots=postgresql-16#event_source), [17](../param-reporting-logging-where-log.md?pivots=postgresql-17#event_source), [18](../param-reporting-logging-where-log.md?pivots=postgresql-18#event_source)                                                                                                 | Sets the application name used to identify PostgreSQL messages in the event log.|
| `log_destination`          | [11](../param-reporting-logging-where-log.md?pivots=postgresql-11#log_destination), [12](../param-reporting-logging-where-log.md?pivots=postgresql-12#log_destination), [13](../param-reporting-logging-where-log.md?pivots=postgresql-13#log_destination), [14](../param-reporting-logging-where-log.md?pivots=postgresql-14#log_destination), [15](../param-reporting-logging-where-log.md?pivots=postgresql-15#log_destination), [16](../param-reporting-logging-where-log.md?pivots=postgresql-16#log_destination), [17](../param-reporting-logging-where-log.md?pivots=postgresql-17#log_destination), [18](../param-reporting-logging-where-log.md?pivots=postgresql-18#log_destination)                                                                         | Sets the destination for server log output. Valid values are combinations of \"stderr\", \"syslog\", \"csvlog\", \"jsonlog\", and \"eventlog\", depending on the platform.|
| `log_directory`            | [11](../param-reporting-logging-where-log.md?pivots=postgresql-11#log_directory), [12](../param-reporting-logging-where-log.md?pivots=postgresql-12#log_directory), [13](../param-reporting-logging-where-log.md?pivots=postgresql-13#log_directory), [14](../param-reporting-logging-where-log.md?pivots=postgresql-14#log_directory), [15](../param-reporting-logging-where-log.md?pivots=postgresql-15#log_directory), [16](../param-reporting-logging-where-log.md?pivots=postgresql-16#log_directory), [17](../param-reporting-logging-where-log.md?pivots=postgresql-17#log_directory), [18](../param-reporting-logging-where-log.md?pivots=postgresql-18#log_directory)                                                                                         | Sets the destination directory for log files. Can be specified as relative to the data directory or as absolute path.|

|-------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `allow_alter_system`    | [17](../param-version-platform-compatibility-platforms-clients.md?pivots=postgresql-17#allow_alter_system), [18](../param-version-platform-compatibility-platforms-clients.md?pivots=postgresql-18#allow_alter_system)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 | Allows running the ALTER SYSTEM command. Can be set to off for environments where global configuration changes should be made using a different method.|
| `transform_null_equals` | [11](../param-version-platform-compatibility-platforms-clients.md?pivots=postgresql-11#transform_null_equals), [12](../param-version-platform-compatibility-platforms-clients.md?pivots=postgresql-12#transform_null_equals), [13](../param-version-platform-compatibility-platforms-clients.md?pivots=postgresql-13#transform_null_equals), [14](../param-version-platform-compatibility-platforms-clients.md?pivots=postgresql-14#transform_null_equals), [15](../param-version-platform-compatibility-platforms-clients.md?pivots=postgresql-15#transform_null_equals), [16](../param-version-platform-compatibility-platforms-clients.md?pivots=postgresql-16#transform_null_equals), [17](../param-version-platform-compatibility-platforms-clients.md?pivots=postgresql-17#transform_null_equals), [18](../param-version-platform-compatibility-platforms-clients.md?pivots=postgresql-18#transform_null_equals) | Treats \"expr=NULL\" as \"expr IS NULL\". When turned on, expressions of the form expr = NULL (or NULL = expr) are treated as expr IS NULL, that is, they return true if expr evaluates to the null value, and false otherwise. The correct behavior of expr = NULL is to always return null (unknown).|

| `archive_library` | [15](../param-write-ahead-log-archiving.md?pivots=postgresql-15#archive_library), [16](../param-write-ahead-log-archiving.md?pivots=postgresql-16#archive_library), [17](../param-write-ahead-log-archiving.md?pivots=postgresql-17#archive_library), [18](../param-write-ahead-log-archiving.md?pivots=postgresql-18#archive_library)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         | Sets the library that will be called to archive a WAL file. ### Write-Ahead Log / Settings



|           Name           |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            Versions                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                                                                                                                                                                    Description                                                                                                                                                                    |
|--------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `commit_delay`           | [11](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-11#commit_delay), [12](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-12#commit_delay), [13](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-13#commit_delay), [14](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-14#commit_delay), [15](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-15#commit_delay), [16](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-16#commit_delay), [17](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-17#commit_delay), [18](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-18#commit_delay)                                                                                 | Sets the delay in microseconds between transaction commit and flushing WAL to disk.|
| `commit_siblings`        | [11](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-11#commit_siblings), [12](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-12#commit_siblings), [13](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-13#commit_siblings), [14](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-14#commit_siblings), [15](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-15#commit_siblings), [16](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-16#commit_siblings), [17](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-17#commit_siblings), [18](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-18#commit_siblings)                                                         | Sets the minimum number of concurrent open transactions required before performing \"commit_delay\".|
| `fsync`                  | [11](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-11#fsync), [12](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-12#fsync), [13](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-13#fsync), [14](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-14#fsync), [15](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-15#fsync), [16](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-16#fsync), [17](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-17#fsync), [18](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-18#fsync)                                                                                                                                         | Forces synchronization of updates to disk. The server will use the fsync() system call in several places to make sure that updates are physically written to disk. This ensures that a database cluster will recover to a consistent state after an operating system or hardware crash.|
| `full_page_writes`       | [11](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-11#full_page_writes), [12](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-12#full_page_writes), [13](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-13#full_page_writes), [14](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-14#full_page_writes), [15](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-15#full_page_writes), [16](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-16#full_page_writes), [17](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-17#full_page_writes), [18](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-18#full_page_writes)                                                 | Writes full pages to WAL when first modified after a checkpoint. A page write in process during an operating system crash might be only partially written to disk. During recovery, the row changes stored in WAL are not enough to recover. This option writes pages when first modified after a checkpoint to WAL so full recovery is possible.|
| `synchronous_commit`     | [11](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-11#synchronous_commit), [12](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-12#synchronous_commit), [13](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-13#synchronous_commit), [14](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-14#synchronous_commit), [15](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-15#synchronous_commit), [16](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-16#synchronous_commit), [17](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-17#synchronous_commit), [18](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-18#synchronous_commit)                                 | Sets the current transaction's synchronization level.|
| `wal_buffers`            | [11](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-11#wal_buffers), [12](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-12#wal_buffers), [13](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-13#wal_buffers), [14](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-14#wal_buffers), [15](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-15#wal_buffers), [16](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-16#wal_buffers), [17](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-17#wal_buffers), [18](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-18#wal_buffers)                                                                                         | Sets the number of disk-page buffers in shared memory for WAL. Specify -1 to have this value determined as a fraction of shared_buffers.|
| `wal_compression`        | [11](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-11#wal_compression), [12](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-12#wal_compression), [13](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-13#wal_compression), [14](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-14#wal_compression), [15](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-15#wal_compression), [16](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-16#wal_compression), [17](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-17#wal_compression), [18](../param-write-ahead-log-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-18#wal_compression)                                                         | Compresses full-page writes written in WAL file.|
